<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><b>Item 5.07 Submission of Matters to a Vote of Security Holders</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: left; margin: 0pt 0">At the 2021 Annual Meeting of Shareholders of the Company held on May&#160;11,
2021, the votes cast with respect to each item of business properly presented at the meeting are as follows:</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: left; margin: 0pt 0">Proposal No.&#160;1 &#8212; The shareholders elected each of the twelve
nominees to the Board of Directors for a one-year term by the vote of the majority of votes cast, in accordance with 3M&#8217;s Bylaws.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Proposal No.5 &#8212; The shareholders did not approve the shareholder
proposal on setting target amounts for CEO compensation.*</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">*Under the General Corporation Law of the State of Delaware, the affirmative
&#8220;FOR&#8221; vote of a majority of those shares present in person or represented by proxy at the meeting and entitled to vote on
the matter is required to approve the shareholder proposal. In tabulating the voting result, abstentions and, if applicable, broker non-votes
are not counted as votes &#8220;FOR&#8221; or &#8220;AGAINST&#8221; the proposal. An abstention will, however, be counted as entitled
to vote on a proposal and will, therefore, have the effect of a vote &#8220;AGAINST.&#8221;&#160; Applying this standard, the percentage
in favor of the shareholder proposal is calculated by dividing the number of FOR votes by the sum of the number of FOR, AGAINST and ABSTAIN
votes.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>
